Lobby: At the entrance, there is a concierge to help open the car door and take the luggage, and take it to the front desk to check in. The front desk warmly welcomes and upgrades the room. The scenery is unbeatable. The front desk manager Li Miao took the initiative to add WeChat when he saw that it was the first time to come, and sent a fruit plate. Introduce the hotel information and send it to the room. During the stay, ask if there are any needs at any time. Check-out was delayed to 2 pm and sent off in the lobby. Butler service.
Facilities: The hotel has a swimming pool
The heated swimming pool is less crowded and comfortable
After swimming, you can go to the steam room to relax. Please note that you need to bring your own swimming cap when entering the swimming pool
There are also shops on site where you can buy swimming caps
There are also gyms, yoga rooms, children's playrooms, etc. for different groups of people
Lobby lounge: Two drink coupons are given upon check-in
You can exchange coffee, juice and other drinks in the lounge. The spiral staircase in the lounge is a popular photo spot for Internet celebrities
The room is spacious enough
Open the door and the curtains and lights will open automatically
The bed is comfortable and you can choose your own pillow
The soundproofing is good and it is very quiet at night
Free drip coffee and tea bags are provided in the room
The bathroom is equipped with byredo brand toiletries
Breakfast: The buffet breakfast has a variety of options
The overall taste is good and I am full. They will also provide guests with freshly baked egg tarts. In short, this experience is very good and I will continue to come back

Address: Building 4, International Trade Center, No. 1 Hongfu East Road, Dongcheng Street, Dongguan

Transportation: Take the high-speed rail to Dongguan Station/Humen Station, take the subway to Hongfu Road Metro Station, and walk about five minutes to arrive
The overall design of the hotel is in Lingnan style. Although the lobby is not large, the white magnolia crystal tree at the entrance attracts people's attention at once. I saw the good young lady checking in and taking pictures. The design of the concierge desk and the front desk is also very distinctive.
The spiral staircase in the lobby lounge is very photogenic. There are two a**ospheres during the day and at night, and there are live bands at night.
The basic room area booked this time is 45 square meters. There is a piece of wood at the door. It is very interesting. I asked the hotel and it was said to be the "Guangzhou Fragrance" with Dongguan characteristics. The room also shows the design of Lingnan characteristics everywhere.

There are 2 restaurants. The Western restaurant buffet dinner is online. The variety of French oysters is very good. There are also dishes delivered for dinner.

The only drawback is that the signage in the mall is not clear, and I had to go around in a long circle to finally enter the hotel after exiting the mall.
The design of the hotel lobby draws on the Lingnan characteristics, a layout of "pavilions high, buildings in the middle, and rooms low". The door is not big. After entering, you can see the magnolia flower installation art embedded in the wall in the center, which is the city flower of Dongguan.
The background wall of the lobby adopts the wok-ear style, which rises and falls one after another, adding a formal sense of Guancheng culture to the space.
The left side of the lobby is the front desk, and the right side is the executive lounge. The overall sense of space in the lobby is very strong, drawing on key elements such as Keyuan, Guancao, Lingnan Painting School and Huangqi Mountain. The executive lounge has a resident band performance in the evening, showing the resonance of Lingnan culture and modern exquisite life.
The design of the room is also full of a combination of simplicity and modernity, with Lingnan gardens as the design moving line. The background of the bedside is cleverly integrated into the weaving elements of corolla, which stretches and is blown low by the wind. The toiletries are all BYREDO, and the details are well done. However, the view outside the window is a construction site. There is no construction yet, and there is no noise. It just looks bare.

We have stayed in many hotels. In recent years, many five-star hotels have tampered with the category of buffet breakfast, reducing expensive ingredients, or only providing expensive ingredients in the executive lounge. But this hotel is very authentic in that respect. At the same time, the hotel food delivery service category is also very rich.

In terms of service, the service personnel of the hotel are very meticulous and professional, and the training is in place.

The only flaw is the hotel swimming pool (I heard from friends that it may be outsourced). There is a swimming coach Payton who is very good. I guess he was assigned to do boring lifeguard work. The same swimming pool service, Ritz-Carlton has done a good job, it is recommended to visit.

The flaws are not hidden, I still think InterContinental is the most worthwhile hotel to stay in Dongguan when traveling.

The hotel‚Äôs breakfast is on the first floor, and the choice of dishes is very rich. I stayed for two days and ate every morning and ate different things. There are many types of Western-style bread and pastries. Chinese meals such as glutinous rice chicken, dim sum, raw claypot porridge, and Dongguan roast goose noodles can be eaten for breakfast. Breakfast is better than many five-star hotels.

When I checked in, the little brother at the front desk strongly recommended me to go to the swimming pool, so I bought a set on Jingdong that day without a swimsuit. The special thing about the hotel swimming pool is that the side of the swimming pool is transparent, and you can see everyone's swimming in the pool standing next to it. I was the only one to get there at 8:15 in the morning. I would like to mention that the dressing room of the swimming pool is very well designed and spacious. The arrangement of lockers, dressing rooms, and shower rooms makes people feel organized. The young lady in charge of registration will always be there to ensure your safety while you are swimming. In addition, after I finished swimming, my little sister told me that the sauna room was opened for me, and the service was very attentive.

Because I am a member of IHG, the hotel also sent two welcome drink coupons on the day of check-in. You can redeem coffee, juice, beer and other beverages in the lobby on the first floor. If the check-in day is not very full, you can also apply for a late check-out, many details are satisfactory.

If you come to Dongguan, regardless of business trip or family trip, you may wish to consider living in Dongguan InterContinental.
